-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `playerlog`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `playerlog` (
  `id` int(8) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `player` int(8) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('coach','ageYear','form','stamina','experience','keeper','defender','playmaker','winger','passing','scorer','setPieces') NOT NULL,
  `old` int(8) NOT NULL,
  `new` int(8) NOT NULL,
  `date` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
